RemoteGraph\n\n\u003e **Class** in `langgraph`\n\n📖 [View in docs](https://reference.langchain.com/python/langgraph/pregel/remote/RemoteGraph)\n\nThe `RemoteGraph` class is a client implementation for calling remote\nAPIs that implement the LangGraph Server API specification.\n\nFor example, the `RemoteGraph` class can be used to call APIs from deployments\non LangSmith Deployment.\n\n`RemoteGraph` behaves the same way as a `Graph` and can be used directly as\na node in another `Graph`.\n\n## Signature\n\n```python\nRemoteGraph(\n    self,\n    assistant_id: str,\n    /,\n    *,\n    url: str | None = None,\n    api_key: str | None = None,\n    headers: dict[str, str] | None = None,\n    client: LangGraphClient | None = None,\n    sync_client: SyncLangGraphClient | None = None,\n    config: RunnableConfig | None = None,\n    name: str | None = None,\n    distributed_tracing: bool = False,\n)\n```\n\n## Parameters\n\n| Name | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `assistant_id` | `str` | Yes | The assistant ID or graph name of the remote graph to use. |\n| `url` | `str \\| None` | No | The URL of the remote API. (default: `None`) |\n| `api_key` | `str \\| None` | No | The API key to use for authentication. If not provided, it will be read from the environment (`LANGGRAPH_API_KEY`, `LANGSMITH_API_KEY`, or `LANGCHAIN_API_KEY`). (default: `None`) |\n| `headers` | `dict[str, str] \\| None` | No | Additional headers to include in the requests. (default: `None`) |\n| `client` | `LangGraphClient \\| None` | No | A `LangGraphClient` instance to use instead of creating a default client. (default: `None`) |\n| `sync_client` | `SyncLangGraphClient \\| None` | No | A `SyncLangGraphClient` instance to use instead of creating a default client. (default: `None`) |\n| `config` | `RunnableConfig \\| None` | No | An optional `RunnableConfig` instance with additional configuration. (default: `None`) |\n| `name` | `str \\| None` | No | Human-readable name to attach to the RemoteGraph instance. This is useful for adding `RemoteGraph` as a subgraph via `graph.add_node(remote_graph)`. If not provided, defaults to the assistant ID. (default: `None`) |\n| `distributed_tracing` | `bool` | No | Whether to enable sending LangSmith distributed tracing headers. (default: `False`) |\n\n## Extends\n\n- `PregelProtocol`\n\n## Constructors\n\n```python\n__init__(\n    self,\n    assistant_id: str,\n    /,\n    *,\n    url: str | None = None,\n    api_key: str | None = None,\n    headers: dict[str, str] | None = None,\n    client: LangGraphClient | None = None,\n    sync_client: SyncLangGraphClient | None = None,\n    config: RunnableConfig | None = None,\n    name: str | None = None,\n    distributed_tracing: bool = False,\n)\n```\n\n| Name | Type |\n|------|------|\n| `assistant_id` | `str` |\n| `url` | `str \\| None` |\n| `api_key` | `str \\| None` |\n| `headers` | `dict[str, str] \\| None` |\n| `client` | `LangGraphClient \\| None` |\n| `sync_client` | `SyncLangGraphClient \\| None` |\n| `config` | `RunnableConfig \\| None` |\n| `name` | `str \\| None` |\n| `distributed_tracing` | `bool` |\n\n\n## Properties\n\n- `assistant_id`\n- `name`\n- `config`\n- `distributed_tracing`\n- `client`\n- `sync_client`\n\n## Methods\n\n- <code>POST /runs/stream</code> otherwise.</p></div></div></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="tabler-icon tabler-icon-chevron-right h-4 w-4 text-foreground-muted group-hover:text-foreground-secondary shrink-0 transition-colors"><path d="M9 6l6 6l-6 6"></path></svg></a></div><script>$RS("S:80","P:80")</script><div hidden id="S:81"><a id="member-stream_events-14" class="group relative flex items-start gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg border border-border bg-background-secondary hover:border-gray-300 dark:hover:border-white/20 hover:bg-gray-50 dark:hover:bg-white/5 transition-colors" style="cursor:pointer" href="/python/langgraph/pregel/remote/RemoteGraph/stream_events"><span class="px-2 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium rounded shrink-0 mt-0.5 bg-teal-100 text-teal-800 dark:bg-teal-900 dark:text-teal-200">method</span><div class="flex-1 min-w-0"><div class="flex items-baseline gap-2 flex-wrap"><span class="font-mono text-foreground group-hover:text-foreground transition-colors">stream_events</span></div><div class="mt-1 [&amp;_code]:text-xs text-foreground-secondary line-clamp-2"><div class="markdown-content markdown-compact "><p class="text-sm m-0">Stream events from this remote graph.</p>

text-lg"><p>The <code>RemoteGraph</code> class is a client implementation for calling remote
APIs that implement the LangGraph Server API specification.</p>
<p>For example, the <code>RemoteGraph</code> class can be used to call APIs from deployments
on LangSmith Deployment.</p>
<p><code>RemoteGraph</code> behaves the same way as a <code>Graph</code> and can be used directly as
a node in another <code>Graph</code>.</p></div></div><script>$RS("S:2","P:2")</script><div hidden id="S:86"><div class="markdown-content markdown-compact "><p>Additional headers to include in the requests.</p></div></div><script>$RS("S:86","P:86")</script><div hidden id="S:87"><div class="markdown-content markdown-compact "><p>A <code>LangGraphClient</code> instance to use instead of creating a default client.</p></div></div><script>$RS("S:87","P:87")</script><div hidden id="S:88"><div class="markdown-content markdown-compact "><p>A <code>SyncLangGraphClient</code> instance to use instead of creating a default client.</p></div></div><script>$RS("S:88","P:88")</script><div hidden id="S:89"><div class="markdown-content markdown-compact "><p>An optional <code>RunnableConfig</code> instance with additional configuration.</p></div></div><script>$RS("S:89","P:89")</script><div hidden id="S:8a"><div class="markdown-content markdown-compact "><p>Human-readable name to attach to the RemoteGraph instance.
This is useful for adding <code>RemoteGraph</code> as a subgraph via <code>graph.add_node(remote_graph)</code>.
If not provided, defaults to the assistant ID.</p></div></div><script>$RS("S:8a","P:8a")</script><div hidden id="S:8b"><div class="markdown-content markdown-compact "><p>Whether to enable sending LangSmith distributed tracing headers.</p></div></div><script>$RS("S:8b","P:8b")</script><script>$RB=[];$RV=function(a){$RT=performance.now();for(var b=0;b<a.length;b+=2){var c=a[b],e=a[b+1];null!==e.parentNode&&e.parentNode.removeChild(e);var f=c.parentNode;if(f){var g=c.previousSibling,h=0;do{if(c&&8===c.nodeType){var d=c.data;if("/$"===d||"/&"===d)if(0===h)break;else h--;else"$"!==d&&"$?"!==d&&"$~"!==d&&"$!"!==d&&"&"!==d||h++}d=c.nextSibling;f.removeChild(c);c=d}while(c);for(;e.firstChild;)f.insertBefore(e.firstChild,c);g.data="$";g._reactRetry&&requestAnimationFrame(g._reactRetry)}}a.length=0};
